<clause id="cls-1" type="scope" obligation="normative">
<title>Scope</title>
<p id="_ab28fb11-e5bd-ffbc-2e46-207f6c65db0f">This OGC Standard for Designing and Writing Modular Standards, also known as the <tt>ModSpec</tt>:</p>

<ul id="_c8c40b5a-3342-c347-9470-9934f13b73a6"> <li> <p id="_901e1445-2ed9-5758-1b98-ff4dfb370bc0">Specifies rules for the internal structure and organization of a standard.</p>

000729cls-8
Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="cls-8" obligation="normative">
<title>ModSpec Requirements Class: Core</title>
<p id="_ab14847c-a247-8411-8f76-b20319f63d93">This clause specifies the requirements, recommendations, and permissions for the content and structure of a modular standard.
This collection of requirements, recommendations, and permissions are also known as the <tt>core</tt> of the ModSpec.
All the requirements specified in this ModSpec core comprise the ModSpec Core Requirements Class.</p>
2



000735cls-8-1
Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="cls-8-1" obligation="normative">
<title>General Requirements</title>
<p id="_20c6ed46-7def-86f1-f44d-2f66281d0970">The following requirement states that every requirement in a standards document is associated with one and only one requirements class(es).</p>

<requirement id="req-0" model="ogc"> <identifier>/req/core/reqs-are-in-class</identifier> <component class="part"> <p id="_d3a9b970-f6b5-2579-81e5-7bfc1c781119">Each requirement in a standard <em>SHALL</em> be associated with exactly one requirements class.</p>
2

001096req-13
